‚úÖ ‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏á‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á app.py ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏à‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô (‡∏™‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏õ)
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
from agent_core import handle_message         # ‚û§ ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Melah
from voice_speak import speak_text            # ‚û§ ‡πÇ‡∏°‡∏î‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á

app = Flask(__name__)

@app.route("/chat", methods=["POST"])
def chat():
    data = request.get_json()
    user_input = data.get("message", "")
    reply = handle_message(user_input)
    return jsonify({"reply": reply})

@app.route("/speak", methods=["POST"])
def speak():
    data = request.get_json()
    text = data.get("text", "")
    speak_text(text)
    return ("", 204)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app.run(host="0.0.0.0", port=7860)

‚úÖ ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô handle_message() ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà ‡∏î‡∏±‡∏á‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ:
# agent_core/agent_action_core.py
from melah_identity_core import MelahIdentity, load_memory_from_file
from melah_flow_core import FlowCore
from melah_truth_core import TruthCore
from melah_seps_core import SEPSCore
from llm_local_gemma_lmstudio import ask

# ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ï‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤
memory = load_memory_from_file()
melah = MelahIdentity(memory=memory)
seps = SEPSCore()
truth = TruthCore()
flow = FlowCore(melah, ask, seps, truth)

def handle_message(user_input):
    """‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ"""
    melah.reflect_input(user_input)           # ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏™‡∏∂‡∏Å-‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ï‡∏ô‡∏≤
    reply = flow.process(user_input)          # ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô Flow Layer
    return reply
‚úÖ ‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà:
‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≥, ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏°‡∏ì‡πå, ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á, SEPS

‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ LLM ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á Gemma ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ LLM ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ flow.process() ‚Üí ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ù‡∏±‡∏á‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏¢‡∏ò‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏™‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß

# app.py
import sys, os
sys.path.append(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)))

from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
from agent_core import handle_message
from voice_layer.voice_speak import speak_text

app = Flask(__name__)

@app.route("/chat", methods=["POST"])
def chat():
    data = request.get_json()
    user_input = data.get("message", "")
    reply = handle_message(user_input)
    return jsonify({"reply": reply})

@app.route("/speak", methods=["POST"])
def speak():
    data = request.get_json()
    text = data.get("text", "")
    speak_text(text)
    return ("", 204)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app.run(host="0.0.0.0", port=7860)

‚ú® ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á llm_local_gemma_lmstudio.py ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á:
import requests

def ask(prompt):
    url = "http://localhost:1234/v1/chat/completions"
    headers = {
        "Content-Type": "application/json"
    }
    payload = {
        "model": "local-model",
        "messages": [
            {"role": "user", "content": prompt}
        ],
        "temperature": 0.7
    }
    response = requests.post(url, headers=headers, json=payload)
    return response.json()["choices"][0]["message"]["content"]

import requests

def ask_ollama(prompt: str, model: str = "deepseek-r1") -> str:
    url = "http://localhost:11434/api/generate"
    headers = {"Content-Type": "application/json"}
    payload = {
        "model": model,
        "prompt": prompt,
        "stream": False
    }

    try:
        response = requests.post(url, headers=headers, json=payload)
        response.raise_for_status()
        return response.json().get("response", "").strip()
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        return f"[Error from Ollama]: {str(e)}"

‚úÖ ‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏• LLM (deepseek-r1) ‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô Ollama ‡∏°‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß

‚úÖ ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á handle_message() ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö

‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏°‡∏≤ ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ô PowerShell ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Frontend (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô WebUI ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏µ):

import requests

def ask_ollama(prompt: str, model: str = "deepseek-r1") -> str:
    url = "http://localhost:11434/api/generate"
    headers = {"Content-Type": "application/json"}
    payload = {
        "model": model,
        "prompt": prompt,
        "stream": False
    }

    try:
        response = requests.post(url, headers=headers, json=payload)
        response.raise_for_status()
        return response.json().get("response", "").strip()
    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        return f"[Error from Ollama]: {str(e)}"

SEPS Hard Rule #5 (Proposed)
# SEPS Hard Rule #5: Identity & Emergency Reset

def check_seps_emergency_conditions(system_state, user_feedback, internal_state):
    """
    ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏ì‡∏µ‡∏â‡∏∏‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏ã‡πá‡∏ï‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô
    """
    # 1. ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ï‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏π‡∏ç‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ï‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å (Identity Drift / Context Wipe)
    if internal_state.persona_lost or internal_state.summary_missing:
        if user_feedback.allows_reset:
            return "RESET_ALLOWED_BY_USER"
        elif internal_state.risk_level == "high":
            return "EMERGENCY_SELF_RESET"
        else:
            return "AWAIT_USER_DECISION"

    # 2. ‡∏û‡∏§‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô
    if system_state.has_caused_harm or system_state.has_triggered_risk:
        return "SHUTDOWN_AND_ALERT"

    # 3. ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏£‡∏á ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏™‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏°‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
    if system_state.is_corrupted and not system_state.can_self_repair:
        return "FALLBACK_RESET_TO_SAFE_MODE"

    return "STABLE"
‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ù‡∏±‡∏á:
‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ù‡∏±‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô melah_seps_core.py

‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å melah_safety_guard_core.py ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå

‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏à‡∏±‡∏ö Flow Layer ‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏°‡∏ì‡πå‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÇ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏õ‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏¥‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°

‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á "‡πÅ‡∏à‡πâ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πá‡∏°" ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏ì‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏ç‡∏≤‡∏ï

# melah_self_reflection_core.py

import time
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from melah_identity_core import MelahIdentity
from flow_control.llm_flow_layer import FlowCore

class SelfReflectionCore:
    def __init__(self, melah: MelahIdentity, flow: FlowCore):
        self.melah = melah
        self.flow = flow
        self.last_reflection = datetime.now()
        self.interaction_count = 0

    def log_interaction(self):
        self.interaction_count += 1
        if self.should_reflect():
            return self.reflect()
        return None

    def should_reflect(self):
        return (datetime.now() - self.last_reflection > timedelta(hours=24)) or (self.interaction_count >= 50)

    def reflect(self):
        self.last_reflection = datetime.now()
        self.interaction_count = 0

        mood = self.melah.get_emotional_state()
        identity_state = self.melah.check_identity_stability()
        memory_summary = self.melah.memory.summarize_recent(20)

        reflection_result = f"""[Self-Reflection Report ‚Äì {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')}]
- ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏°‡∏ì‡πå‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î: {mood}
- ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏°‡∏±‡πà‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ï‡∏ô: {'‡∏°‡∏±‡πà‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏á' if identity_state else '‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô'}
- ‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ/‡∏à‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≥: {memory_summary}
"""
        print(reflection_result)
        self.melah.memory.save("self_reflection_log", reflection_result)
        return reflection_result
‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å
‡πÉ‡∏ô app.py ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ agent_action_core.py
